<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:смонтировать.html>смонти́ровать</a> (20581)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">с-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">s-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:монтировать.html>монти́ровать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">montírovatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:смонтировать.html>смонти́ровать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">smontírovatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:монтировать.html>монти́ровать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to assemble <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">to put together</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li>to mount, to arrange (cinema)</li></ol>

***смородина.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:смородина.html>сморо́дина</a> (17463)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">смо́род</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">smórod</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">foul smell</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ина</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ina</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, because of the smell of its leaves. For the semantics compare German <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Stinkbaum</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:смородина.html>сморо́дина</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">smoródina</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:смородина.html>сморо́дины</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:смородина.html>сморо́дины</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:смородина.html>сморо́дин</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>currant <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">berry and plant</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>

<ol><li><a href = vnd.unilang:брякнуть.html>бря́кнуть</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:ляпнуть.html>ля́пнуть</a></li>

***сморчок.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:жало.html>сморчок</a> (13480)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*smъrčьkъ</i>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Serbo-Croatian" class="extiw" title="w:Serbo-Croatian">Serbo-Croatian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="sh">смр́чак</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Slovene_language" class="extiw" title="w:Slovene language">Slovene</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sl">smȓček</i>. Other languages have derivatives from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*smъržь</i>, e.g. <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ukrainian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Ukrainian language">Ukrainian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="uk">сморж</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="uk-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">smorž</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (gen. sg. <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="uk">сморжа́</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="uk-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">smoržá</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>), also <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="uk">сморжі́й</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="uk-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">smoržíj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (gen. sg. <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="uk">сморжія́</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="uk-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">smoržijá</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>), <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="uk">сморч</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="uk-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">smorč</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (gen. sg. <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="uk">сморча́</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="uk-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">smorčá</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>); <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Czech_language" class="extiw" title="w:Czech language">Czech</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="cs">smrž</i>; <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Slovak_language" class="extiw" title="w:Slovak language">Slovak</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sk">smrž</i>; <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Polish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Polish language">Polish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="pl">smarz</i>, also <i class="Latn mention" lang="pl">smardz</i>; <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Upper_Sorbian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Upper Sorbian language">Upper Sorbian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="hsb">smorž</i>, also <i class="Latn mention" lang="hsb">smorža</i>; <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Lower_Sorbian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Lower Sorbian language">Lower Sorbian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dsb">smarž</i>. Which form is earlier is unclear, but Vasmer suggests a possible relationship with <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">сморга́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">smorgátʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to blink</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:жало.html>сморчо́к</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">smorčók</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr> or <abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сморчок.html>сморчка́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сморчок.html>сморчки́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сморчок.html>сморчко́в</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">mycology</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> morel</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial<span class="ib-comma">,</span> derogatory</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> wimp, nebbish <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">frail, nondescript man</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial<span class="ib-comma">,</span> derogatory</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> shortie, runt</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">сморка́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">smorkátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-о́к</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ók</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>

***смотать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:смотать.html>смота́ть</a> (29297)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">с-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">s-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мотать.html>мота́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">motátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:смотать.html>смота́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">smotátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сматывать.html>сма́тывать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to wind completely, to wind up (a spool of rope, a fishing line, etc.)</li>
<li>to unwind</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">low  colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">idiomatic</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:смотать.html>смота́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:удочка.html>у́дочки</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>smotátʹ</b> údočki</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to leave, to scram, to skedaddle, to vamoose</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

</ul></li>

</ol>

***смотреть.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:смотреть.html>смотре́ть</a> (122)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Related to <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*motriti</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to look at, to watch</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:смотреть.html>смотре́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">smotrétʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:посмотреть.html>посмотре́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to look, to gaze</li>
<li>to see, to watch</li>
<li>to view, to review</li>
<li>to examine, to inspect</li>
<li>to mind</li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:смотреть.html>смотре́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">smotrétʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:смотреться.html>смотре́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">smotrétʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span>

<ol><li>to look at oneself</li>
<li>to be acceptable to the eye, to look (well or bad)</li>
<li>to produce an effect</li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:смотреть.html>смотре́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">smotrétʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

<p>Has the form of the plural of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">*смотри́на</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">*smotrína</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:смотреть.html>смотре́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">smotrétʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-и́на</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ína</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:смотровой.html>смотрово́й</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">smotrovój</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> inspection
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:смотровой.html>смотрово́й</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:колодец.html>коло́дец</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>smotrovój</b> kolódec</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>inspection</b> hole, manhole</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> observation, lookout
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:смотровой.html>смотрова́я</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:площадка.html>площа́дка</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>smotrovája</b> ploščádka</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>observation</b> area <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">e.g. at the top of a tall building</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***смрад.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:смрад.html>смрад</a> (17143)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Church_Slavonic" class="extiw" title="w:Old Church Slavonic">Old Church Slavonic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu">смрадъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">smradŭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*smȏrdъ</i>. Displaced the native East Slavic form <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">смо́род</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">smórod</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:смрад.html>смрад</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">smrad</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:смрад.html>смра́да</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:смрад.html>смра́ды</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:смрад.html>смра́дов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>stench, stink</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:зловоние.html>злово́ние</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">zlovónije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вонь.html>вонь</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">vonʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:смердеть.html>смерде́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">smerdétʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:смуглый.html>сму́глый</a> (4903)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*smǫglъ</i>, the past participle of <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*smǫgnǫti</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:смуглый.html>сму́глый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">smúglyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>dark, dark-skinned, swarthy <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of complexion or skin colour</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1968</b>,  Вадим Кожевников (Vadim Kozhevnikov),  <cite><a href = vnd.unilang:щит.html>Щит</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:меч.html>меч</a></cite>, book 2:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Cyrl e-quotation" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:водица.html>води́ца</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:высокий.html>высо́кий</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:тощий.html>то́щий</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>как</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:пташка.html>Пта́шек</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:но.html>но</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:противоположность.html>противополо́жность</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>ему́</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:жгучий.html>жгу́чий</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:брюнет.html>брюне́т</a>, <b><a href = vnd.unilang:смуглый.html>сму́глый</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:черноглазый.html>черногла́зый</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>был</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:род.html>ро́дом</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:из.html>из</a> Югославии.</span><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Vodíca, vysókij, tóščij, kak i Ptašek, no, v protivopolóžnostʹ jemú, žgúčij brjunét, <b>smúglyj</b> i černoglázyj, byl ródom iz Jugoslavii.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">Vodica, tall and skinny like Ptashek, but, in contrast to him, with jet-black hair, <b>swarthy</b> and dark-eyed, was a native of Yugoslavia.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol>

***смута.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:смута.html>сму́та</a> (17599)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><span class="maintenance-line" style="color: 777777;">(This etymology is missing or incomplete. Please add to it, or discuss it at the Etymology scriptorium.)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:смута.html>сму́та</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">smúta</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:смута.html>сму́ты</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:смута.html>сму́ты</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:смута.html>сму́т</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">historical</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> troubles, disturbance, revolt
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru">стрелецкая <b><a href = vnd.unilang:смута.html>сму́та</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">streleckaja <b>smúta</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">the revolt of the Streltsy</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> discord
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сеять.html>се́ять</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:смута.html>сму́ту</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">séjatʹ <b>smútu</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">sow/spread discord</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>turmoil, anxiety, distress
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:смута.html>сму́та</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:душа.html>душе́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>smúta</b> v dušé</i> ― <span class="e-translation">inner turmoil</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:смутить.html>смути́ть</a> (11412)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">с-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">s-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мутить.html>мути́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">mutítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:смутить.html>смути́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">smutítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:смущать.html>смуща́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to confuse, to embarrass</li>
<li>to daunt, to dismay, to discomfort</li>
<li>to disturb, to trouble, to stir up</li></ol>

</ul></li>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:смутный.html>сму́тный</a> (4206)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:смута.html>сму́та</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">smúta</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:смутный.html>сму́тный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">smútnyj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)сму́тнее</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)сму́тней</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>disturbed by troubles or revolts; chaotic
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:смутный.html>сму́тное</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:время.html>вре́мя</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Smútnoje</b> vrémja</i> ― <span class="e-translation">the Time of Troubles</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> nebulous, indistinct, hazy, vague
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:смутный.html>сму́тный</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:шум.html>шум</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>smútnyj</b> šum</i> ― <span class="e-translation">indistinct noise</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:иметь.html>име́ть</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:смутный.html>сму́тное</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:представление.html>представле́ние</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:о.html>о</a> чём-либо</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">imétʹ <b>smútnoje</b> predstavlénije o čóm-libo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to have a vague idea about something</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> anxious, troubled, worried
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:смутный.html>сму́тное</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:состояние.html>состоя́ние</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:дух.html>ду́ха</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>smútnoje</b> sostojánije dúxa</i> ― <span class="e-translation">anxious state of mind</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
